<rate>5</rate><Text>An old-school shop, with an old-school proprietor to help and repair just about anything.  Very honest, very reasonable and 100% unvarnished bicycle culture.

This is not a fancy shop. There are no nice displays, there's not any good lighting, it's frankly a mess. This is where you go to get a great deal on a used bike, to get something fixed quickly and competently when other shops would tell you to throw it away, to meet a mechanic that can not only fix that old part but that has spares for it. This is the type of shop where you can shake the mechanic's greasy hand, feel good about the impact that a six-pack of beer can have for a job well done, ask the owner to teach your son how to change his own tire, meet bicycle riders who ride for fun and never, ever really see anybody wearing lycra...haha!

The proprietor of this shop really knows his stuff and did an excellent job at repairing my older bicycle. He will patiently answer your questions and give you a breakdown of the work he has done. Please do keep in mind the following, though. He does not repair ebikes. < Review>
Mari Kimbap shop is an excellent spot to check out if you're looking for a cute place to grab simple, bite-sized Kimbap and not feel too full after finishing your meal. I love how most of their Kimbap options are set-up entree style where you can pick the meats you want for you and your friends. It's nice having variety instead of being stuck with the same Kimbap for the full meal. Best of all each Kimbap is the same price and if you order at least $10 you can use their yelp check in offer for another Kimbap for free! Highly recommend this place if you're looking for a light meal.<//Review>

The staff are super helpful, and the store is pretty clean and organized. Some tips for shopping here. Deliveries and returns have always been pretty easy and straight forward.
1. Always do some research first, they will price match to meet competition.
2. Don't pay sticker price, use promotions to get the best deal.
3. Always communicate with the staff, and try to haggle a deal if your on the fence about the purchase.

Horrible management aka Perry Thomas!

On 12/23/18 I purchased just over $2700 from the Ashley's Furniture Store in Fairfield Ca. Where I payed in full and in cash. That day I scheduled a delivery for 2/15/19. About a week and a half before my delivery date I called the customer care number to push back my delivery to 2/23/19 since the remolding of both  my bathrooms & new flooring weren't completed. On 2/13/19 I get a text saying I need to confirm my confirmation of delivery for the 2/15/19 or else my furniture won't be placed on the truck. Well, why would it? I had called a week & a half earlier to change the delivery date. When I called customer care back they stated that, that wasn't done but they could reschedule then. So she rescheduled for 2/23/19. On 2/21/19 I received another text stating I needed to confirm delivery for 2/23/19 or call customer care to reschedule. I had to call customer care because my bathrooms we're now completed but the flooring was still unfinished. So, I pushed it back to 3/13/19. On 3/11/19 I should of received a text saying I needed to confirm delivery but I received nothing. I called that night after I got off work but they we're already closed. I called the next day only to find out there was no delivery set up for the 13th. A day in which I took off of work in order to be home so I could receive my furniture.
